<user_id>102893546445623108723</user_id><username>Jonathan Nowlan</username><Date>1532200306934</Date><rating>2< /rating>< Text>
I'll start this review with the good stuff. The lady who assisted me was great. While my overall experience at this location was not positive I could tell she was doing the best she could with a bad situation. I wish I remembered her name because she deserves a raise.

Now for the bad stuff. This location is only open till noon on Saturdays which causes a big back log of people needing to pick up up their rentals and also people needing to return their rentals. It took me an hour to get my car since they ran out of cars and were waiting for people to do returns so they could immediately give those cars out to at least a dozen people who were waiting in the small location office.

The staff did the best they could with the limited resources they had and they were able to deal with irritated customers in a professional manner.

My advice to the public would be to avoid renting from this location on a Saturday or if you have to make the reservation for Saturday, make it as early as possible in the day.

My advice to the management of this location would be to consider leaving the office open an extra few hours on Saturdays to prevent these sorts of backlogs.

Last note, while they didn't have the time to fully detail the car before giving it to me it was clean and it worked perfectly.

Cheers.</Text>

<Text>Just a complete rip-off!!! I brought my vehicle in for a smog, they said it failed. When I went to pay for it they referred me to some ATS automotive. This is a test only location, so they are not allowed to make referrals as it can be a conflict of interest. I didn't go to the place they referred me too, and instead I went to Auto Express, a much better and much more honest mechanic that also does smog. I had him check out my car and he found nothing wrong with it. He ran emissions tests on it twice and told me that there should be no problem passing it. So I brought it back to AD smog because they had offered me $10 off a retest (even though the sign on the wall inside says the first retest is free) and it failed again. So I immediately brought it over to Auto Express and he had him smog it. It passed with flying colors. When I inquired what was going on, he told me that AD smog must be measuring emissions while the vehicle is cold, a practice that is not supposed to happen and often results in an unwarranted failed test. AD smog was able to get $110 out of me for smog tests and made an illegal referral to another business that I assume they are hoping will also benefit from this arrangement they have. Total scam here, don't bring your vehicle to dishonest people. I should not fail a test at one location, drive 3 blocks and then pass the test at another location. Bill J.

This is probably the worst quality food and customer service I have ever experienced. The old lady who owns the shop refused to remake my smoothie because she was stuck on the difference of whether I ordered a smoothie or Energy smoothie. It's literally the same thing.

I ordered a banana and peanut butter smoothie, and when I got it it tasted like a macchiato. And I simply I want a peanut butter smoothie not coffee. And the young lady who took the order apologized and said the owner rather give you your money back. Which I then said, "can't you just remake it ?" And she said yes, then came back and said the owner would rather give you your money back.

And I said okay...and she still didn't want to give me my money back.

I've been coming here for 10+ years, and I should have noticed with all the differences, that it's owned by someone completely new.

This old lady raised the prices, doesn't speak English, and insists that the customer is wrong if you question the quality of food or if the order is correct.

I can't believe she was arguing back and forth with me in front of her employee with other customers in line.
She obviously doesn't care about her customers or the quality of her food.

Save yourself a walk on this block and avoid her cafe at all costs.< /text>
